# Comments for Question 3, LLM=Grok 3 Mini Beta (low)

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.3)
    The pattern recognition center during naptime creates an effective, distinctive atmosphere of hushed isolation. The stained glass lamp serves as both a physical and symbolic focal point, casting meaningful "mocking rainbows" that enhance the tone. The digital abyss where the monster lurks connects well with the setting's technological nature. However, sensory details beyond visual elements are limited, missing opportunities to deepen immersion through sound, texture, or other sensations.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=8.1)
    The abandoned spaceport customs office with its humming server rooms creates a compelling juxtaposition of futuristic technology and ancient family traditions. The atmosphere of isolation and mechanical persistence effectively mirrors Elara's emotional state. Sensory details like the "incessant hum" and "mechanical heartbeat" create an immersive environment that enhances the themes of rigidity versus elasticity. The setting's emptiness powerfully reinforces her isolation.
